<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=telephone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/telephone" class="extiw" title="w:telephone">telephone</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/telephone" class="extiw" title="w:telephone">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Dialog_gr_1972.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Dialog_gr_1972.jpg/220px-Dialog_gr_1972.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="161" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Dialog_gr_1972.jpg/330px-Dialog_gr_1972.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Dialog_gr_1972.jpg/440px-Dialog_gr_1972.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2044" data-file-height="1500"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Dialog_gr_1972.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A rotary-dial telephone</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=telephone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>First used by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Graham_Bell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Graham Bell">Alexander Graham Bell</a> in 1876 to refer to the modern instrument, but previous devices had been given this name, which was borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/t%C3%A9l%C3%A9phone#French" title="téléphone">téléphone</a></i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CF%84%E1%BF%86%CE%BB%CE%B5#Ancient_Greek" title="τῆλε">τῆλε</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">têle</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">afar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CF%86%CF%89%CE%BD%CE%AE#Ancient_Greek" title="φωνή">φωνή</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phōnḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">voice, sound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=telephone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈ tɛl.ɪˌfəʊn/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ˈ tɛl.əˌfəʊn/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈ tɛl.əˌfoʊn/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=telephone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">telephone</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/telephones#English" title="telephones">telephones</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/telecommunication" title="telecommunication">telecommunication</a> <a href="/wiki/device" title="device">device</a> (originally <a href="/wiki/mechanical" title="mechanical">mechanical</a>, and now <a href="/wiki/electronic" title="electronic">electronic</a>) used for two-way talking with another person (now often shortened to <a href="/wiki/phone" title="phone">phone</a>).
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonyms&nbsp;▲</a></span><span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>hyponym&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blower#English" title="blower">blower</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/phone#English" title="phone">phone</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/farspeaker#English" title="farspeaker">farspeaker</a></span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Ameche#English" title="Ameche">Ameche</a></span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/dog_and_bone#English" title="dog and bone">dog and bone</a></span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/horn#English" title="horn">horn</a></span>; <i>see also</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:phone" title="Thesaurus:phone">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">phone</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym" style="display: none;"><span class="defdate">Hyponym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cellphone#English" title="cellphone">cellphone</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/American_English" title="American English">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The game of <a href="/wiki/Chinese_whispers" title="Chinese whispers">Chinese whispers</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> October 27,  Erik Adams,  “TV: Review: THE SIMPSONS (CLASSIC): “The PTA Disbands””, in  <cite>The Onion AV Club</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.avclub.com/articles/the-pta-disbands,104762/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And since the spring of 1995, no game of <b>telephone</b> has ended without some Simpsons-loving smart-ass dropping “purple monkey dishwasher” into the chain.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/American_English" title="American English">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Chinese_whispers" title="Chinese whispers">Chinese whispers</a>; a situation in which an initial message has been distorted and misunderstood by being passed from person to person.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b> October 3,  David Dobbs,  “The Touch of Madness”, in  <cite>Pacific Standard</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://psmag.com/magazine/the-touch-of-madness-mental-health-schizophrenia">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In other words, Jones' career and life may have been derailed because a game of <b>telephone</b> went bad.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=telephone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">telephone</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/telephones#English" title="telephones">telephones</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/telephoning#English" title="telephoning">telephoning</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/telephoned#English" title="telephoned">telephoned</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/transitive" title="transitive">transitive</a>, <a href="/wiki/intransitive" title="intransitive">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (attempt to) contact someone using the telephone.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barr_(writer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barr (writer)">Robert Barr</a>,  chapter 4, in  <cite>Lord Stranleigh Abroad</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1796924W">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“I came down like a wolf on the fold, didn’t I ?  Why didn’t I <b>telephone</b> ?  Strategy, my dear boy, strategy. This is a surprise attack, and I’d no wish that the garrison, forewarned, should escape. …”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1961</b> November,  “Talking of Trains: Derailment near Holmes Chapel”, in  <cite>Trains Illustrated</cite>, page 652:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The length ganger saw the train passing with the van derailed and promptly <b>telephoned</b> the <a href="/wiki/Sandbach#English" title="Sandbach">Sandbach</a> signalman, who restored his signals to danger, but not in time to stop the train before the final derailment occurred.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To convey (a message) by telephoning.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2012</b>, Robert Byron, ‎Jan Morris, <i>Europe in the Looking-Glass</i>
<dl><dd>David <b>telephoned</b> his apologies to his mother.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
